Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Reverend Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from heaven at the age of 16, has lived his entire life centered solely on the heavenly way! He described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any wealth, it is nothing but the suffering endured for the public good rather than for myself. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. …… Reverend Moon has been opposed and persecuted by countless people from nations and the world until now. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. Never in history has the world united to attack and eliminate one person like this. In that sense, Reverend Moon is a global champion.
However, despite being cursed, I did not crumble or collapse. I came out even stronger without the slightest tremor. …… Reverend Moon insists on liberating humanity, the spiritual world, hell, and even God." (Refer to Collected Speeches, Vol. 105, pp. 101-103)
In a word, Reverend Moon's life can be defined as 'suffering itself.' The nature of this suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. Here, we come to know who he is. Reverend Moon came as the Second Coming, the Messiah, and the True Parent of humanity, whom Christianity has hoped for over 2,000 years. Already, disciples following him in 185 countries around the world are realizing the ideal of the true family to walk the path of true children with such a confession of faith.
Reverend Moon's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humans, history, and the world are clarified within his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled within him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, more importantly, Reverend Moon's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, incarnate. Therefore, life itself is truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'words.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through Reverend Moon's words. The realm of his words is so high and deep that it cannot be fully comprehended, but it fundamentally has three characteristics.
First, through his words and life, Reverend Moon revealed God. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the lineage of evil, they are children yet cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. Reverend Moon made God 'speak' despite being tragically alienated by human sin. He made God, who was silent and trapped in church authority, doctrine, and ornate buildings, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' making Reverend Moon 'the perfect revelation of God.'
Secondly, Reverend Moon liberated humans from ignorance and chaos. We humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, yet we cannot deny the tragic reality of not fully understanding our own existence. Moreover, despite being interdependent beings inseparable from others, we have not clarified that relationship. This is because we lost God's words. Reverend Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Furthermore, through a life that upholds the heavenly way, he shows a concrete exemplary path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Reverend Moon liberated the world of all things. Every creation made by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully realized under the original dominion of humans, it has not been, causing all things to groan. Reverend Moon revealed the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Reverend Moon and his wife, who came as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly speak around the world today, demonstrating with their substantial lives the teachings of 'serve with the heart of a parent and the body of a servant' and 'live for the sake of others,' striving to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Moreover, through his words of life, noble life, and achievements, Reverend Moon has ultimately restored God's sovereignty as we welcome the new millennium, settling as the King of Blessed Families on this earth. He is creating the Peace UN, binding the world into one realm of heart, aiming for Cheon Il Guk, the Fourth Israel, the Kingdom of Peace.
I hope that the esteemed readers who encounter these words will also become owners of Cheon Il Guk and become protagonists in building the Kingdom of Peace. *

So the mother must make Cain and Abel one. Then she must serve Adam. There can be no self-assertion. 
When you realize that the subject authority has been reversed, you must unite centered on the husband. If it becomes insufficient, the mother must discuss with the father and say, 'This is right.' That's how it should be. Isn't that the principle? In this way, you must influence your sons. It's a formula. You can't live as if the world is living on its own. You must create a way of living, writing down the names of your children, and making them unite with someone. 
You too. To lead a church, you must center on those who came to the church first and those who came later, and bind them as Cain and Abel. Isn't that right? Raise them that way. You don't do that, do you? You have to pair them up when they come in. Then why do they fall away? The reason so many people have fallen away from the Unification Church until now is because of these leaders. Because they only care for themselves. You too. You can't do without friends. You need friends in social life. Word friends, witnessing friends, event friends. When holding an event, it's someone, and when discussing words, it's someone else. You must plan like that, select yourself, and think of a way to grow by connecting with people from a subject standard. Because the word is the best, you must read it day and night, and stand in the position of either the subject or the object in front of that standard. 
Even while listening to these words, think, 'Why did the teacher say this?' When speaking, evaluate by thinking, 'The person who listens is worse than me, so they are worth listening to.' When praising, think, 'Ah, if they are better than me, I should praise them.' You must attend this reading session, this gathering with such a mindset. 
What does it matter if you attend for a thousand years? If you can't compare and absorb the good and bad, what does it matter? It's a waste of time, a waste of space, and air pollution. It's not good just because many come. It's that serious. You can't live recklessly throughout your life.

Heaven is where two people are united
Now, what is today's title? Is it the world or the universe? "It's the universe." It would be better if it were world peace and unification, but what is the universe? The universe! 'Universe' consists of 'heaven' (天) and 'house' (宙), meaning house.

When we talk about heaven, we know it as something infinitely wide, infinitely large, and indescribable, but it is simple. What is heaven? Isn't it literally the character 'heaven' (天) where two (二) people (人) are united? Two people are united forever and ever... Looking at God's attributes, since He is absolute, unique, unchanging, and eternal, He is absolute, unique, unchanging, and eternal. If there is love between the two, He is the king of love; if there is happiness, He is the king of happiness; if there is peace, He is the king of peace. As the ideal subject, from the unity of the two, the world is seen as a creation world that has developed and expanded from small to large.

Therefore, if you exclude the two, a complete one... When there are two, there is no concept of one. Isn't that right? When there are two, there is no concept of one. Then what creates the concept of one? This is the problem. What is the desire we seek in this world today? We say we need money, knowledge, and power. Then is it possible to unite two people with money? With knowledge? With power?

Everyone, when it comes to power, there is no flexibility or harmony in the relationship between superiors and subordinates. There is no unified peace. What about knowledge? Even when scholars gather for many conferences, when they gather, they claim to be the top based on who knows more about their specialized field. They say, "Listen to me!" There can be no unity there.

Then money! Can you unite with money? Even if a couple is exemplary and model-like, today, they have separate bank accounts. How about you? How about the elders here, from the president to the vice mayor? When it comes to money, they put it in their own pockets, lock it with iron, hang it under their name, and fight to the death over it. In such a world, is there a concept of two becoming one? This is a serious issue, although it seems simple. There isn't.

Peace with money? Hmm. (Shakes head) Peace with knowledge? Hmm. (Shakes head) Then with politics? Hmm. (Shakes head) Have you thought about it, elders?

Then what can make two become one? The character 'heaven' (天) is where two (二) people (人) are united. Isn't it two people? In Confucianism, it is said, "Originality, prosperity, benefit, and correctness are the constants of the heavenly way, and benevolence, righteousness, propriety, and wisdom are the principles of human nature." The character for benevolence (仁) itself is two (二) people (亻). I would like to talk more, but due to time constraints, let's leave it at that. The ideal, happy, free, and liberating totality of the subject where two people are absolutely, uniquely, unchangingly, and eternally united is heaven.

The universe is structured in pairs to become one through love
In this way, all things created in relation to heaven are not alone. You see your face every day, don't you? How many parts are there on your face? There are four. How many are there in total? Seven. One, two, three, four, five, six, seven. Seven are united, but does the face, representing the five senses, do whatever it wants?

The right eye and the left eye are relative. If the right eye goes up, the left follows, doesn't it? Does it say, "Hey right eye, you go up, I'll go down"? Does the right nostril and the left nostril breathe separately? How stuffy is it when one nostril is blocked due to a cold? Looking at this, even the way our face is formed is all about harmony for unity, for the completion and perfection of my life itself.

Isn't it the same with arms and legs? Do they do whatever they want? If the right hand reaches for something, the left follows. They all cooperate. The feet do the same. Although they move oppositely, they cooperate. There is nothing that deviates from the official counterpart ideology, that's how it is seen.

From this perspective, how is the universe structured? The conclusion is that it is structured in pairs! Say it once. "It is structured in pairs!" It's a precious word, pairs. Isn't it so these days? Even bacteria that can only be seen when magnified millions of times are said to have male and female.

Then why is the universe structured in pairs? "It became as it wanted." It became as it wanted, but what is the content of both wanting to become? To become one, to become one. Everything starts from becoming one, and when complete things unite with larger things, they create even larger complete things. This is the theoretical conclusion. We exist in pairs to become one, with what? God's love! You must know this. God's love! It's not human love.

Christians talk about love centered on Christianity, and Buddhists talk about compassion. Isn't compassion the same? What is the character for compassion (慈)? It's two '玄' characters with a heart (心), what is this? It speaks of two counterparts becoming one. There, the heart must become one. Compassion is also love. The fact that everything is based on love and makes it the fundamental desire of all is for unity! With whom? With whom? With my five senses, with my limbs.

Looking at the limbs, do you have the concept of 'I'? That concept of 'I', did you know that even you yourself are made of a body and mind that are two in one? They are two in one. If there is a conflict there, if there is mental suffering, it has a greater impact than being sick. They must become one. They must become one.

Even all my five senses and limbs move as one based on a relative relationship. When we see this, our internal self and external self must become one. The internal self is invisible. The external self is visible, but it must become one with the invisible. With what? It's the same. Love.

When you receive your parents' love, both your mind and body feel good. You seek a place of love where both your body and mind can feel good.

Who is the subject when it comes to body and mind?
When viewed from this perspective, even from an individual's standpoint, there must be a duality of character, a plus character and a minus form, whether in a vertical-horizontal relationship or a horizontal-horizontal relationship, or in a front-back relationship, centered on a relative content, they must become one. The more complex it is, the greater the power of love that can unite complex things, the more it is great love. It is great love, infinite love. The main body of that is none other than God. You must know that it is not human. Even if humans desire an ideal world, a dream world, a utopia, it is impossible with humans.

Isn't human love like that? When you look at humans, no matter how big they are, if they are a spring, how much water can they pump out? Only God, who is the fundamental being that moves this great universe, can pump out infinitely, infinitely, infinitely, and continue to do so, and no matter how much He nurtures, it doesn't decrease, always maintaining the same content, and having a continuous relationship with us, can determine unchanging peace, unchanging love, and unchanging ideals. This is theoretical.

Then do you understand what the universe is? It refers to a house where two people live. Your body is also a country where two people live, isn't it? Therefore, in the Bible, in 1 Corinthians 3:16, it says, "Don't you know that your body is a temple?" It is God's house. It is God's house. God's masculine nature is divided. It is not thesis-antithesis-synthesis (正反合). The communist ideological world is thesis-antithesis-synthesis, but there is no way for synthesis to occur from antithesis. It is thesis-division-synthesis (正分合) logic. The philosophical basis is fundamentally different.

From this perspective, when you look at your body and mind, who is the subject? This is the problem. Is the body the subject, or is the mind the subject? In this universe, is the visible world the subject, or if there is an invisible God, is the invisible God the subject? Even if you establish a relationship centered on your individual self and expand it to the great universe, it must be able to return.

It must be able to return after starting from the individual. For that to happen, everything must be orderly. There must be no conflicting existence. What can make that possible? Love. Greater love! Greater love returns quickly.

Then if there is God, what is God's love? It is not our individual love. It is not the love of 40 million people in Korea, these days 47 million? What do you estimate? "Yes, it is 47 million." I thought it was less than 45 million, but it has become 47 million. It grows well! (Laughter) If it exceeds 50 million, becomes 100 million, and becomes the largest country in the world... Even if the land is small, it would be a concern if it becomes a large country. How nice would it be if our ancestors had settled in a country like Brazil? 8 billion people can live in South America. Wow, why didn't they settle in such a land, and why did they remain in a small peninsula called Samcheolli, unfortunately?

Even if people living on Earth knew the spirit world... How vast is the spirit world? In our galaxy, where the solar system is located, there are hundreds of billions of stars, and in the great universe, there are 100 billion systems like the solar system. Wow! It's unimaginable. 100 billion. Even 1,000 is a lot, but 100 billion? Such a vast world couldn't have just appeared. It exists centered on movement. It must be moving in a subject-object relationship for thousands of years. Even looking at just the Earth, they say it is over 4 billion years old, but does it deviate by one second in its rotation? Thinking it happened naturally is madness. If you trace the origin and explain all that, it would be good, but there is no time.

Happiness lies in two people living for each other
So, everything is trying to unite and live happily. Then our vice mayor says, "I am happy." Are you happy now? The people of Daegu look up to the vice mayor, but what is the limit of that happiness? That's how it is. What has been the issue with Reverend Moon in the world so far? The problem of the world is the two people, the man and the woman. The world has become complicated because of the problem of two people. Isn't Daegu complicated? Even just the city. When you dig into the complex issues, it is the problem of two people. If two people could have been happy without being a problem, what would have happened? The problem lies there. If two people lived for each other, if they said they live for each other, could they be happy or not? "They could be happy."

The president and the vice mayor here are the same. Three people, four people, even ten people, if ten people live for each other, would they be unhappy, or would there be no unhappy person? Then it keeps going up. It's about living for others. It's about development. When you say live for others, you are pulling all ten people, so it keeps decreasing. Eventually, there will be none left.

Everything is simple. How can the world be happy? "I will live for everything, with the universe, with this existing world. Since I do, you do too. Let the mind do so, and let the body do so." This is it. The body and mind are different, aren't they? The body does what the body wants, and the mind does what the mind wants. Why is that? Because it deviated from the path of living for others.

When a man and a woman get married, they love each other like a pair of doves, but these days, what is a week? There are cases where they divorce right after leaving the wedding hall, in places like America. I've seen it a lot. My goodness! Who do you trust? Love that cannot overcome death cannot connect to God's love
Two people completely united and living together is the universe! Heaven or earth, such people can make it their home and live happily and peacefully forever. Would God be there or not? He is all there.

Because he conducted reconciliation movements in the interreligious aspect and transcended nations in the international aspect, unless you deny that, his achievements stand on a global standard, even if history doesn't want to place him there. Isn't that right?

Jesus loved his enemies, and because of that love, Jesus' thought surpassed the world. Even enemies. What is the thought of the Unification Church's teacher? Those who can marry with a heart of loving enemies go to the highest heaven. They don't know that. Japanese women! Japanese men! Try doing it your way.

So what did the teacher say? From now on, those who had international marriages, those who married enemies, those people will be mainly used. In the future, Korean-Korean married people might not be used. The era where those who had international marriages succeed has come. Isn't that right? You have to know that.

That's why people who want to be famous in their country and graduated from such schools won't be used. Those who graduated from schools established by the teacher will be used in the future. Those who had international marriages are studying. Isn't that right? It's the same with Sun Moon University. I established middle and high schools. Even Bridgeport. I even established kindergartens. Sun Moon University doesn't have a high school, right? The president didn't come today. Is there a high school? "No." We need to create one.

If university professors teach high school students, they boast. Do you understand? How proud and hard they will study. Smart students, even if they are in the third year, if they are smart, they can enter university and study. We can educate geniuses. I'm thinking of creating such a school. Now! (Continued reading)

"It's finished." Who will pray? Pray. (Chairman Hwang Sun-jo's prayer)

Achieve your liberation realm

After proclaiming the Cheonju Peace Unification Kingdom and establishing the victory foundation of the fourth Adam realm, having set all the blessed families of all nations and peoples in such a position is fulfilling the teacher's responsibility. There is nothing to demand from the teacher. Neither God, humanity, nor the nation. Isn't that right? You have to know that.

This is not a coincidence. You have to think that it came about under a predetermined plan. That's why these three or four years are precious. Do you understand? "Yes." You must find the nation. Didn't you all pledge? "Yes."

Now, with your roots in your hometown.... If it's Yoo Jong-gwan, continue and revive the connections from past gatherings and places where you held events, and reconnect them. Do you understand? "Yes." You were a district leader, right? "Yes." Go to your hometown and find the direction related to it, the places you flew to, like geese crossing the ocean and continents, and start from there to bear fruit from all the past experiences, transferring the victory you achieved to that place. Now, should you find your hometown or not? "I should go." Do as you please.

That's why if it's Hwang Sun-jo, if you do that, you can set up your wife or your siblings, educate them, and do everything. Then automatically, the responsibility of that family can be replaced, and it spreads sideways. That's how it connects to the nation. Don't let go.

World leaders should send their relatives to replace them if they can't be there themselves, making sure they can act as substitutes. Even if someone else becomes the leader, by standing in the position of a deputy leader supporting them, because the roots and branches are extended there, flowers and fruits cannot fail to bloom and bear fruit. Flowers will bloom, and fruits can be borne anywhere. Do you understand? Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes." Don't discard it.

That's why the teacher is helping those who came out of Pyongyang this time. The success of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is not for himself but for the world. To make it a global success, it must be connected with history. Do you understand?

That's why I even bought pearl gifts in Hawaii for those who graduated from Ewha Women's University. Even those who opposed us. They don't know why they did it, but they did it. But you have to pity their children at least. It's the third generation, the third generation. From the perspective of a meritorious subject, you have to think of the third generation, and even if the main ancestor disappeared in the middle, you have to pass on the merit to them. I've been doing that all along.

Once this is over, what do you do? From the 36 families of the Unification Church, there are all sorts of people, right? Educate them two or three times. We educated them recently, right? "Yes." To go beyond this, if you can't go, you have to follow your wife's family. If there's a mother-in-law, follow her out. Follow your mother-in-law and gather at her house. Do you understand?

If you couldn't evangelize, work quickly and do more than the Unification Church members, and the environment will naturally absorb you. You have to plan for your survival. Otherwise, you can't come directly here. You'll feel sorry to see the teacher. How much the teacher suffered and worked hard during that time. So you....

That's why the clan is good. If the clan matches that, and if the clan does several times more than the person in charge, naturally, relatives will connect and come and go, achieving their liberation realm.

That's why you shouldn't give up the past. You have to settle the past. If you owe a debt, you have to repay it. That's why Unification Church members must do that. Those who have been around for a long time must do that. If you met the teacher and received the blessing, you shouldn't just use it; you have to establish a position. In that sense, whether you look east, west, north, south, up, down, front, back, left, or right, you must be a fruit without any hindrance. You must be a fruit that has done everything to reinforce it, to become a seed that can be eternal.

That's why God doesn't lose history. Although thousands of years have passed from the past to now, He revives it all, blesses those who worked hard, resurrects them, and fills the positions, even finding those in hell and filling heaven, making it all fit perfectly. You can't give up on it.

So those who owe a debt and betray will face the beginning of night wherever they go. Didn't you owe a lot to the Unification Church? Did you owe the teacher or not? "We did." Those who sit on it and want to enjoy luxury, the world won't allow it. Knowing that, the fourth Adam realm! "Yes." The teacher has planted seeds in good soil. Knowing that.... (Bowing) *
